			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {has_idea = sunni}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = RULE_SALAFIST_BRANCH
						option = yes  
					}
				}
				add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = 0.025 }
				if = {
					limit = {has_government = democratic}
					start_civil_war = {
						ideology  = democratic
						ruling_party = fascism
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {has_government = communism}
					start_civil_war = {
						ideology  = communism
						ruling_party = fascism
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {has_government = neutrality}
					start_civil_war = {
						ideology  = neutrality
						ruling_party = fascism
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {has_government = nationalist}

						ideology  = nationalist
						ruling_party = fascism
					}

					limit = {has_idea =  shia}
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = shia
						add_idea  = sunni
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {has_idea =  sufi_islam}
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = sufi_islam
						add_idea  = sunni
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {has_idea =  ibadi}
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = ibadi
						add_idea  = sunni
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {has_idea =  christian}
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = christian
						add_idea  = sunni
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {has_idea =  orthodox_christian}
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = orthodox_christian
						add_idea  = sunni
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {has_idea =  pluralist}
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = pluralist
						add_idea  = sunni
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {has_idea =  buddism}
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = buddism
						add_idea  = sunni
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {has_idea =  hindu}
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = hindu
						add_idea  = sunni
					}
				}

		x = 6
		y = 0

		cost = 10

		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus czechia_international_diplomacy"
			if = { limit = { has_government = democratic }
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_government = fascism }
						NOT = { has_government = nationalist }
						NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
						has_opinion = { target = ROOT value > -25 }
						OR = {
							is_neighbor_of = ROOT
							has_government = democratic
						}
					}
					add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = political_outreach }
				}
			}
			else_if = { limit = { has_government = fascism }
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
						has_opinion = { target = ROOT value > -25 }
						OR = {
							is_neighbor_of = ROOT
							has_government = fascism
						}
					}

				}
			}
			else_if = { limit = { has_government = neutrality }

							is_neighbor_of = ROOT
							has_government = neutrality

						NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
						has_opinion = { target = ROOT value > -25 }

			factor = 1
		}

	focus = {
		id = czechia_focus_ModerateMuslim
		icon = umocr
		x = 53
		y = 9
		#relative_position_id = czechia_unite_against_them
		
		cost = 0.15
		
		allow_branch = {
			has_country_flag = czechia_tree_muslim
		}
		search_filters = {FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL}
		prerequisite = { }
		mutually_exclusive = { focus = czechia_focus_caliphate }
		available = {
			has_government = fascism
		}
		historical_ai = { }
		select_effect = { }
		bypass = { }
		cancel = { }

		cancel_if_invalid = yes
		continue_if_invalid = no
		available_if_capitulated = no
		
		complete_tooltip = { }
		completion_reward = {
			add_political_power = 150

			set_temp_variable = { czechia_muslims_ammount = var:party_popularity@fascism }
			add_to_temp_variable = { czechia_muslims_ammount = var:party_popularity@neutrality }
			multiply_temp_variable = { czechia_muslims_ammount = 100 }

			set_temp_variable = { czechia_dem_ammount = var:party_popularity@democratic }
			multiply_temp_variable = { czechia_dem_ammount = 100 }

			set_temp_variable = { czechia_com_ammount = var:party_popularity@communism }
			multiply_temp_variable = { czechia_com_ammount = 100 }

			set_temp_variable = { czechia_nat_ammount = var:party_popularity@nationalist }
			multiply_temp_variable = { czechia_nat_ammount = 100 }

			set_temp_variable = { czechia_parties_ammount = var:party_popularity@fascism }
			add_to_temp_variable = { czechia_parties_ammount = var:party_popularity@communism }
			add_to_temp_variable = { czechia_parties_ammount = var:party_popularity@democratic }
			add_to_temp_variable = { czechia_parties_ammount = var:party_popularity@neutrality }
			add_to_temp_variable = { czechia_parties_ammount = var:party_popularity@nationalist }
			multiply_temp_variable = { czechia_parties_ammount = 100 }

			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { czechia_parties_ammount < 100 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { czechia_one_ammount = 100 }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { czechia_one_ammount = czechia_parties_ammount }

				set_temp_variable = { czechia_parties_final_ammount = var:czechia_one_ammount }
				add_to_temp_variable = { czechia_parties_final_ammount = var:czechia_muslims_ammount }
				
				hidden_effect = {
					set_popularities = {
						democratic = var:czechia_dem_ammount
						communism = var:czechia_com_ammount
						fascism = 0.0
						neutrality = var:czechia_parties_final_ammount
						nationalist = var:czechia_nat_ammount
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { czechia_parties_ammount = 100 }
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_popularities = {
						democratic = var:czechia_dem_ammount
						communism = var:czechia_com_ammount
						fascism = 0.0
						neutrality = var:czechia_muslims_ammount
						nationalist = var:czechia_nat_ammount
					}
				}
			}

			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 12 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 1 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes

			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
			}
			clear_array = ruling_party
			clear_array = gov_coalition_array
			add_to_array = { ruling_party = 12 }

			if = {
				limit = {
					date < 2008.1.2
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Muhammad Ali Šilhavý"
					picture = "muhammad_ali_silhavy.dds"
					ideology = Neutral_Muslim_Brotherhood
					traits = {
						neutrality_Neutral_Muslim_Brotherhood
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Muneeb Hassan Alrawi"
					picture = "muneeb_alrawi.dds"
					ideology = Neutral_Muslim_Brotherhood
					traits = {
						neutrality_Neutral_Muslim_Brotherhood
					}
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {has_idea =  CZE_mosques_built}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = CZE_mosques_built
					add_idea  = CZE_mosques_built_lite
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {has_idea =  CZE_controlled_news}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = CZE_controlled_news
					add_idea  = CZE_controlled_news_lite
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {has_idea =  CZE_muslim_more_rights}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = CZE_muslim_more_rights
					add_idea  = CZE_muslim_more_rights_lite
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {has_idea =  CZE_muslims_in_army}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = CZE_muslims_in_army
					add_idea  = CZE_muslims_in_army_lite
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {has_idea =  CZE_harsh_caliphate}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = CZE_harsh_caliphate
					add_idea  = CZE_moderate_caliphate
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = czechia_tree_ModerateMuslim
			set_country_flag = czechia_tree1_done_ModerateMuslim
			hidden_effect = {
				add_ideas = { CZ_parties_tree_decision_idea }
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_JIHADISTS
				}
				num_of_civilian_factories > 200
				factor = 4000
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = DEFAULT
				}
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = DEFAULT
				}
				is_historical_focus_on = no
				factor = 1
			}
		}
	}

		id = czechia_focus_libertarian
		icon = svobodni
		x = 44
		y = 10
		#relative_position_id = czechia_unite_against_them
		
		cost = 0.15
		
		allow_branch = {
			has_country_flag = czechia_tree_neutrality
		}
		search_filters = {FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL}
		prerequisite = { focus = czechia_focus_new_parties_neu }
		mutually_exclusive = {
			focus = czechia_focus_green
		}
		available = {
			has_government = neutrality
		}
		historical_ai = { }
		select_effect = { }
		bypass = { }
		cancel = { }

		cancel_if_invalid = yes
		continue_if_invalid = no
		available_if_capitulated = no
		
		complete_tooltip = { }
		completion_reward = {
			add_political_power = 150
			set_country_flag = czechia_tree1_done_libertarian
			hidden_effect = {
				add_ideas = { CZ_parties_tree_decision_idea }
			}
			set_country_flag = czechia_tree_libertarian
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_NEUTRALITY
				}
				factor = 3000
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_NEUTRALITY2
				}
				factor = 3000
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = DEFAULT
				}
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = DEFAULT
				}
				is_historical_focus_on = no
				factor = 1
			}
		}
	}

	focus = {
		id = czechia_focus_libertarian8
		icon = major_alliance
		
		x = 0
		y = 2
		relative_position_id = czechia_focus_libertarian
		
		cost = 5
		
		allow_branch = {
			has_country_flag = czechia_tree_neutrality
		}
		search_filters = {FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL}
		prerequisite = { focus = czechia_focus_libertarian7 }
		mutually_exclusive = {}
		available = {
			has_government = neutrality
			neutrality_neutral_libertarians_are_in_power = yes
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
                tooltip = required_7_focus_libertarian_tt
                has_country_flag = czechia_tree7_done_libertarian
                has_country_flag = czechia_tree_libertarian
            }
		}
		historical_ai = { }
		select_effect = { }
		bypass = { }
		cancel = { }

		cancel_if_invalid = yes
		continue_if_invalid = no
		available_if_capitulated = no
		
		complete_tooltip = { }
		completion_reward = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = czechia_libertarian_rel_with_allies
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_idea = CZ_V4_member
							has_idea = CZ_unofficial_TSI_member
							has_idea = CZ_TSI_member
							has_idea = CZ_CEU_member
						}
					}
					add_opinion_modifier = {
						target = CZE
						modifier = declaration_of_friendship
					}
					CZE = {
						add_opinion_modifier = {
							target = PREV
							modifier = declaration_of_friendship
						}
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = czechia_libertarian_rel_with_allies
			}
			else = {
				add_political_power = 150
			}
			set_country_flag = czechia_tree8_done_libertarian
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_NEUTRALITY
				}
				factor = 3000
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_NEUTRALITY2
				}
				factor = 3000
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = DEFAULT
				}
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = DEFAULT
				}
				is_historical_focus_on = no
				factor = 1
			}
		}
	}
